# FPF-Spec.md Master Index

Pre-built index for FPF-Spec.md. Maps section titles to exact line ranges.
Use line ranges with Read tool (offset/limit) to load specific sections.

## How to use

1. Search this file for keywords related to your topic
2. Find the section with matching keywords
3. Note the Start and End line numbers
4. Read FPF-Spec.md with: offset=Start, limit=(End-Start+1)
